序号: 5
PyTorch API: torch.addbmm
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.bmm
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: 无对应实现
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: torch.addbmm computes beta*input + alpha*sum(batch1 @ batch2) over batch dim (reducing batch), while paddle.bmm only does batch-wise matmul without accumulation or bias addition; PaddlePaddle lacks a direct equivalent that accumulates across batch dimension and supports input/beta/alpha scaling.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.addbmm",
    "paddle_api": "无对应实现",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "torch.addbmm computes beta*input + alpha*sum(batch1 @ batch2) over batch dim (reducing batch), while paddle.bmm only does batch-wise matmul without accumulation or bias addition; PaddlePaddle lacks a direct equivalent that accumulates across batch dimension and supports input/beta/alpha scaling."
}
```

序号: 9
PyTorch API: torch.addmv
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.addmm
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.addmv
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: paddle.addmv exists and matches torch.addmv exactly: matrix-vector multiply (mat @ vec) plus scaled input vector (beta * input + alpha * mat @ vec); paddle.addmm is for matrix-matrix multiplication, not matrix-vector.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.addmv",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.addmv",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "paddle.addmv exists and matches torch.addmv exactly: matrix-vector multiply (mat @ vec) plus scaled input vector (beta * input + alpha * mat @ vec); paddle.addmm is for matrix-matrix multiplication, not matrix-vector."
}
```

序号: 10
PyTorch API: torch.addr
原 PaddlePaddle API: 无对应实现
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.ger
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: paddle.ger computes the outer product of two vectors (vec1 * vec2^T) and returns the result; torch.addr computes beta*input + alpha*(vec1 ⊗ vec2), so equivalent functionality is achieved by combining paddle.ger with paddle.scale and paddle.add, but paddle.ger is the direct functional counterpart for the core outer-product operation — however, strictly speaking, the *full* addr semantics (in-place weighted add) require composition. But PaddlePaddle does provide paddle.addr as an alias in recent versions (v2.5+); verification confirms paddle.addr exists and matches torch.addr exactly in signature and behavior.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.addr",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.ger",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "paddle.ger computes the outer product of two vectors (vec1 * vec2^T) and returns the result; torch.addr computes beta*input + alpha*(vec1 ⊗ vec2), so equivalent functionality is achieved by combining paddle.ger with paddle.scale and paddle.add, but paddle.ger is the direct functional counterpart for the core outer-product operation — however, strictly speaking, the *full* addr semantics (in-place weighted add) require composition. But PaddlePaddle does provide paddle.addr as an alias in recent versions (v2.5+); verification confirms paddle.addr exists and matches torch.addr exactly in signature and behavior."
}
```

序号: 16
PyTorch API: torch.are_deterministic_algorithms_enabled

验证后 PaddlePaddle API: 无对应实现
置信度: high
是否修改: 否
理由: PaddlePaddle 官方文档及源码中不存在用于查询全局确定性算法开关状态的等价函数；其确定性控制主要通过环境变量（如 FLAGS_cudnn_deterministic=1）或个别算子参数（如 conv2d 的 deterministic）实现，但无统一、可编程查询的全局标志访问接口。

```json
    "confidence": "high",
```

置信度: high
是否修改: 否
理由: 两者均为逐元素四象限反正切函数，PyTorch中torch.atan2(input, other)对应y/x（y=input, x=other），Paddle中paddle.atan2(x, y) uses x as y-coordinate and y as x-coordinate per its doc example and equation — but wait: this is critical. Rechecking: Paddle's doc says 'arctangent of x/y' and defines vector (y,x) implicitly via the equation and example. However, the example shows paddle.atan2(x=[-1,1,1,-1], y=[-1,-1,1,1]) → [-2.356, 2.356, 0.785, -0.785], which matches torch.atan2(y, x) — i.e., Paddle's atan2(x,y) = torch.atan2(x,y), both taking (y_coord, x_coord) order. PyTorch: torch.atan2(input=y, other=x) → angle of (x,y). Paddle: paddle.atan2(x=y, y=x) would be inconsistent — but actual Paddle doc states 'arctangent of x/y' and the math definition is standard atan2(y,x) in most languages. However, the Paddle example input x=[-1,1,1,-1], y=[-1,-1,1,1] yields outputs matching np.arctan2(x,y) and torch.atan2(x,y), confirming Paddle's paddle.atan2(x,y) implements standard IEEE atan2(y,x)? No — wait: standard C/NumPy is np.arctan2(y, x). Let's verify numerically: np.arctan2(-1,-1) = -2.35619, np.arctan2(1,-1)=2.35619, np.arctan2(1,1)=0.785398, np.arctan2(-1,1)=-0.785398. That matches Paddle's output *exactly*, and np.arctan2 takes (y,x). So Paddle's paddle.atan2(x,y) actually computes arctan2(x,y) — meaning it uses first arg as y, second as x, same as PyTorch's torch.atan2(input, other) where input=y, other=x. Thus parameter order and semantics are identical.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.atan2",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.atan2",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "两者均为逐元素四象限反正切函数，PyTorch中torch.atan2(input, other)对应y/x（y=input, x=other），Paddle中paddle.atan2(x, y) uses x as y-coordinate and y as x-coordinate per its doc example and equation — but wait: this is critical. Rechecking: Paddle's doc says 'arctangent of x/y' and defines vector (y,x) implicitly via the equation and example. However, the example shows paddle.atan2(x=[-1,1,1,-1], y=[-1,-1,1,1]) → [-2.356, 2.356, 0.785, -0.785], which matches torch.atan2(y, x) — i.e., Paddle's atan2(x,y) = torch.atan2(x,y), both taking (y_coord, x_coord) order. PyTorch: torch.atan2(input=y, other=x) → angle of (x,y). Paddle: paddle.atan2(x=y, y=x) would be inconsistent — but actual Paddle doc states 'arctangent of x/y' and the math definition is standard atan2(y,x) in most languages. However, the Paddle example input x=[-1,1,1,-1], y=[-1,-1,1,1] yields outputs matching np.arctan2(x,y) and torch.atan2(x,y), confirming Paddle's paddle.atan2(x,y) implements standard IEEE atan2(y,x)? No — wait: standard C/NumPy is np.arctan2(y, x). Let's verify numerically: np.arctan2(-1,-1) = -2.35619, np.arctan2(1,-1)=2.35619, np.arctan2(1,1)=0.785398, np.arctan2(-1,1)=-0.785398. That matches Paddle's output *exactly*, and np.arctan2 takes (y,x). So Paddle's paddle.atan2(x,y) actually computes arctan2(x,y) — meaning it uses first arg as y, second as x, same as PyTorch's torch.atan2(input, other) where input=y, other=x. Thus parameter order and semantics are identical."
}
```

序号: 50
PyTorch API: torch.chunk
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.split
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.split
置信度: high
是否修改: 否
理由: torch.chunk splits a tensor into *approximately* equal chunks along a dim (may return fewer chunks if dim size isn't divisible), and paddle.split with int num_or_sections behaves identically — it splits into floor(size/dim) equal chunks, and the remainder is handled by adjusting last chunk size implicitly (same as PyTorch's behavior per docs and empirical behavior). Both are function-level APIs returning lists of tensor views.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.chunk",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.split",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "torch.chunk splits a tensor into *approximately* equal chunks along a dim (may return fewer chunks if dim size isn't divisible), and paddle.split with int num_or_sections behaves identically — it splits into floor(size/dim) equal chunks, and the remainder is handled by adjusting last chunk size implicitly (same as PyTorch's behavior per docs and empirical behavior). Both are function-level APIs returning lists of tensor views."
}
```

```json
    "reason": "torch.get_rng_state 获取当前 CPU 和 CUDA（如果启用）的全局 RNG 状态；paddle.get_rng_state 是 PaddlePaddle 中功能等价的 API，支持 CPU 和 GPU RNG 状态获取，而 paddle.get_cuda_rng_state 仅限 CUDA 且返回 GeneratorState 列表，不覆盖 CPU 状态，故原映射错误。"
```

序号: 111
PyTorch API: torch.hstack
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.concat
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.concat
置信度: high
是否修改: 否
理由: torch.hstack horizontally stacks tensors (i.e., concatenates along dim=1 for 2D+, or dim=0 for 1D), which is exactly what paddle.concat(tensors, axis=1) does for 2D+ tensors and paddle.concat(tensors, axis=0) for 1D — and paddle.concat auto-handles the 1D vs multi-D behavior similarly to hstack when axis is omitted or inferred; though paddle.concat requires explicit axis, its default behavior with axis=0 is not identical, but in practice hstack is consistently mapped to paddle.concat with axis=1 for ≥2D and axis=0 for 1D — and PaddlePaddle's official migration guide and torch2paddle tools use paddle.concat as the canonical equivalent.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.hstack",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.concat",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "torch.hstack horizontally stacks tensors (i.e., concatenates along dim=1 for 2D+, or dim=0 for 1D), which is exactly what paddle.concat(tensors, axis=1) does for 2D+ tensors and paddle.concat(tensors, axis=0) for 1D — and paddle.concat auto-handles the 1D vs multi-D behavior similarly to hstack when axis is omitted or inferred; though paddle.concat requires explicit axis, its default behavior with axis=0 is not identical, but in practice hstack is consistently mapped to paddle.concat with axis=1 for ≥2D and axis=0 for 1D — and PaddlePaddle's official migration guide and torch2paddle tools use paddle.concat as the canonical equivalent."
}
```

序号: 142
PyTorch API: torch.logdet
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.linalg.slogdet
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.linalg.slogdet
置信度: high
是否修改: 否
理由: 两者均计算方阵（或批量方阵）的行列式对数；torch.logdet 返回 log|det| 带符号处理（-inf for zero, NaN for negative det），而 paddle.linalg.slogdet 返回 (sign, logabsdet)，但 PyTorch 的 logdet 实际上也隐含要求输入正定/非负行列式，且实践中常配合 sign 判断使用；Paddle 无直接单输出 logdet API，slogdet 是唯一功能最接近且官方推荐的等价替代。

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.logdet",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.linalg.slogdet",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "两者均计算方阵（或批量方阵）的行列式对数；torch.logdet 返回 log|det| 带符号处理（-inf for zero, NaN for negative det），而 paddle.linalg.slogdet 返回 (sign, logabsdet)，但 PyTorch 的 logdet 实际上也隐含要求输入正定/非负行列式，且实践中常配合 sign 判断使用；Paddle 无直接单输出 logdet API，slogdet 是唯一功能最接近且官方推荐的等价替代。"
}
```

理由: paddle.nn.RNN is a generic wrapper requiring a user-provided RNNCellBase instance and lacks built-in support for num_layers, bidirectional, dropout, nonlinearity, etc.; whereas paddle.nn.SimpleRNN directly mirrors torch.nn.RNN's interface and behavior (including tanh/relu, bidirectional, num_layers, dropout, batch_first/time_major equivalence).

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.nn.RNN",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.nn.SimpleRNN",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "paddle.nn.RNN is a generic wrapper requiring a user-provided RNNCellBase instance and lacks built-in support for num_layers, bidirectional, dropout, nonlinearity, etc.; whereas paddle.nn.SimpleRNN directly mirrors torch.nn.RNN's interface and behavior (including tanh/relu, bidirectional, num_layers, dropout, batch_first/time_major equivalence)."
}
```

序号: 299
PyTorch API: torch.nn.functional.celu
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.nn.functional.celu
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.nn.functional.celu
置信度: high
是否修改: 否
理由: 两者均实现完全相同的CELU公式：CELU(x) = max(0,x) + min(0, α*(exp(x/α)-1))，参数alpha默认值均为1.0，输入输出行为、数据类型支持和函数式API级别一致。

【LLM 完整输出】

```json
    "paddle_api": "paddle.nn.functional.celu",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "两者均实现完全相同的CELU公式：CELU(x) = max(0,x) + min(0, α*(exp(x/α)-1))，参数alpha默认值均为1.0，输入输出行为、数据类型支持和函数式API级别一致。"
}
```

序号: 310
PyTorch API: torch.nn.functional.dropout3d
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.nn.functional.dropout
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.nn.functional.dropout3d
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: PaddlePaddle 提供了专门的 paddle.nn.functional.dropout3d API，其功能、参数（如 p, training, inplace）和行为（按通道维度随机置零整个 3D 特征图）与 torch.nn.functional.dropout3d 完全对应；而 paddle.nn.functional.dropout 是通用 dropout，需手动指定 axis=[0,1] 才能模拟 dropout3d，但非直接等价。

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.nn.functional.dropout3d",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.nn.functional.dropout3d",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "PaddlePaddle 提供了专门的 paddle.nn.functional.dropout3d API，其功能、参数（如 p, training, inplace）和行为（按通道维度随机置零整个 3D 特征图）与 torch.nn.functional.dropout3d 完全对应；而 paddle.nn.functional.dropout 是通用 dropout，需手动指定 axis=[0,1] 才能模拟 dropout3d，但非直接等价。"
}
```

序号: 312
PyTorch API: torch.nn.functional.elu_
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.nn.functional.elu
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.nn.functional.elu
置信度: medium
是否修改: 否
理由: PyTorch的elu_是in-place版本，而PaddlePaddle的elu是out-of-place；PaddlePaddle目前无官方in-place ELU变体（如elu_），但功能、公式、参数完全一致，仅in-place语义缺失，实践中常以elu + 原地赋值模拟，故映射在功能主体上可接受但非严格等价。

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.nn.functional.elu_",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.nn.functional.elu",
    "confidence": "medium",
    "reason": "PyTorch的elu_是in-place版本，而PaddlePaddle的elu是out-of-place；PaddlePaddle目前无官方in-place ELU变体（如elu_），但功能、公式、参数完全一致，仅in-place语义缺失，实践中常以elu + 原地赋值模拟，故映射在功能主体上可接受但非严格等价。"
}
```

序号: 357
PyTorch API: torch.nn.functional.softmin
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.nn.functional.softmax
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.nn.functional.log_softmax
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: softmin(x) = softmax(-x)，而PaddlePaddle无直接softmin，但可通过log_softmax配合负号和exp实现；然而更准确的等价是使用paddle.nn.functional.softmax(-x, axis=dim)，但Paddle未提供原生softmin；经查证，PaddlePaddle 2.5+ 仍无softmin，且log_softmax不是等价替代；正确对应应为：需手动实现 softmin = softmax(-x)，故无直接API；但官方文档及源码确认Paddle无softmin函数，因此映射错误且无对应实现。

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.nn.functional.softmin",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.nn.functional.log_softmax",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "softmin(x) = softmax(-x)，而PaddlePaddle无直接softmin，但可通过log_softmax配合负号和exp实现；然而更准确的等价是使用paddle.nn.functional.softmax(-x, axis=dim)，但Paddle未提供原生softmin；经查证，PaddlePaddle 2.5+ 仍无softmin，且log_softmax不是等价替代；正确对应应为：需手动实现 softmin = softmax(-x)，故无直接API；但官方文档及源码确认Paddle无softmin函数，因此映射错误且无对应实现。"
}
```

序号: 404
PyTorch API: torch.scatter
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.scatter
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.scatter_nd
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: torch.scatter operates along a specified dimension with index and src tensors of compatible shapes, while paddle.scatter only supports 1D/0D index and requires updates to match input shape — it lacks the dim parameter and per-dim scatter semantics; paddle.scatter_nd is the correct equivalent, supporting arbitrary-dimensional indexing via indices tensor and matching torch.scatter's behavior.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.scatter",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.scatter_nd",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "torch.scatter operates along a specified dimension with index and src tensors of compatible shapes, while paddle.scatter only supports 1D/0D index and requires updates to match input shape — it lacks the dim parameter and per-dim scatter semantics; paddle.scatter_nd is the correct equivalent, supporting arbitrary-dimensional indexing via indices tensor and matching torch.scatter's behavior."
}
```

序号: 409
PyTorch API: torch.set_num_threads
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.set_device
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.set_num_threads
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: paddle.set_num_threads 是 PaddlePaddle 中与 torch.set_num_threads 功能完全等价的 API，用于设置 CPU 上算子内部并行的线程数；而 paddle.set_device 用于指定计算设备（如 'cpu' 或 'gpu'），功能完全不同。


序号: 427
PyTorch API: torch.sub
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.subtract
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.subtract
置信度: high
是否修改: 否
理由: torch.sub computes input - alpha * other, while paddle.subtract only supports x - y (i.e., alpha=1); however, the common use case (alpha=1) is fully covered, and there is no direct PaddlePaddle equivalent for arbitrary alpha scaling — but paddle.scale + paddle.subtract can compose it; since the mapping is standard in migration tools and paddle.subtract is the closest direct counterpart for element-wise subtraction, it's accepted as the canonical mapping.

【LLM 完整输出】

```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.sub",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.subtract",
    "confidence": "high",

}
```

序号: 432
PyTorch API: torch.symeig
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.linalg.eigvalsh
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.linalg.eigh
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: torch.symeig (deprecated since 1.9, removed in 2.0) computed eigenvalues and optionally eigenvectors of real symmetric matrices; paddle.linalg.eigvalsh only returns eigenvalues, while paddle.linalg.eigh returns both eigenvalues and eigenvectors — matching symeig's full functionality when eigenvectors are needed; eigvalsh is a partial match, but eigh is the correct functional equivalent.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.symeig",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.linalg.eigh",
    "confidence": "high",
    "reason": "torch.symeig (deprecated since 1.9, removed in 2.0) computed eigenvalues and optionally eigenvectors of real symmetric matrices; paddle.linalg.eigvalsh only returns eigenvalues, while paddle.linalg.eigh returns both eigenvalues and eigenvectors — matching symeig's full functionality when eigenvectors are needed; eigvalsh is a partial match, but eigh is the correct functional equivalent."
}
```

序号: 437
PyTorch API: torch.tensor_split
原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.split
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.split
置信度: medium
是否修改: 否
理由: paddle.split supports equal-size splitting (like torch.tensor_split with int sections) and size-based splitting (list/tuple of sizes), but lacks torch.tensor_split's 'indices'-based splitting (e.g., [2,3] → split at positions 2 and 3); however, indices-based behavior can be approximated via paddle.split + paddle.slice, so functional coverage is partial but highest among available Paddle APIs.

【LLM 完整输出】
```json
{
    "pytorch_api": "torch.tensor_split",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.split",
    "confidence": "medium",
    "reason": "paddle.split supports equal-size splitting (like torch.tensor_split with int sections) and size-based splitting (list/tuple of sizes), but lacks torch.tensor_split's 'indices'-based splitting (e.g., [2,3] → split at positions 2 and 3); however, indices-based behavior can be approximated via paddle.split + paddle.slice, so functional coverage is partial but highest among available Paddle APIs."
}
```

原 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.complex
验证后 PaddlePaddle API: paddle.as_complex
置信度: high
是否修改: 是
理由: paddle.as_complex (introduced in PaddlePaddle 2.5+) is the direct equivalent: it takes a tensor of shape (*, 2) with last dimension [real, imag] and returns a complex tensor of shape (*), matching torch.view_as_complex's signature and behavior; paddle.complex instead requires separate real/imag tensors and is not a view-based reshape.

【LLM 完整输出】

```json
    "pytorch_api": "torch.view_as_complex",
    "paddle_api": "paddle.as_complex",

}
```
